JAN-JUN 1951 RENEWALS

An alphabetical list, by author (artist, or employer in case of a work made for hire) or the renewal claimant in the case of photographic works, of all works of art, scientific and technical drawings, photographic works and prints and pictorial illustrations for which the renewal copyrights were registered during the period covered by this catalog. Information relating to both the original and renewal registration is included in each entry.
